-
-"'''Woman like Me'''" is a song recorded by [[Beyoncé Knowles|Beyoncé]] originally written for and performed in the 2006 film ''[[The Pink Panther (2006 film)|The Pink Panther]]''. Although that version was never released on an album or as a [[single (music)|single]], it was later remixed by [[Steve Austin (rapper)|Steve Austin]] in the album ''Hollywood Cole Presents: I'm the Juggernaut Bitch!''.
-
-==''The Pink Panther''==
-"Woman like Me" was performed [[in character]] by Beyoncé Knowles, as Xania, in two scenes of the 2006 film ''The Pink Panther''.Shuman, I.; Simonds, R., Trench, T. (Producers), & Levy, S. (Director). (2006). ''The Pink Panther''. Los Angeles, CA: Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer. The song was written by Charmelle Cofield, Ron Lawrence, and Beyoncé Knowles. The [[DVD]] version of the film includes an exclusive complete performance of the song in the special features. The song was recorded in [[New York City]] using [[multitrack recording]] where Beyoncé harmonized with herself several times over. Three different [[shot (film)|shot]]s were used from no more than five [[take]]s for the visual performance of the song in the film. Like "[[Check on It]]", "Woman like Me" was not included on the [[The Pink Panther (2006 soundtrack)|soundtrack album for ''The Pink Panther'']].Beck, C. (2006) ''The Pink Panther'' [CD]. Studio City: Varèse Sarabande. The song is not commercially available, but it had an [[Internet leak]].
-
